## HARD CONSTRAINTS (operator-locked, NOT consultable)

  the transport's HTTP client is INJECTED so tests pass an in-process stub (httpx.MockTransport / a
  fake) returning canned responses. No GPU, no Cohere, no Vast, no live endpoint hit in pytest.

## Context — this is M1 of the live-path build (readiness audit 2026-05-29)
The readiness double-check (Claude verify + Codex audit, BOTH NOT_READY) found the 4-role LOGIC is
built + offline-green but the LIVE serving path is unbuilt. M1 is the first live piece: a REAL
`RoleTransport` implementation. The 3 verifier roles (Mirror/Sentinel/Judge) are served on
self-hosted vLLM (per the lock `serving_route: vast_self_host*`); the GENERATOR is NOT in scope —
it already runs live on OpenRouter via `openrouter_client.py` and is upstream of the per-claim
pipeline. So M1's transport serves ONLY mirror/sentinel/judge.

Grounding (read this session, file:line) — REUSE these existing patterns, do NOT reinvent:
- `openrouter_client.py`: request body build (:1389–1502: model/messages/temperature/max_tokens,
  `response_format` json_schema shape :1473–1478, `provider` block :1481–1502), response parse
  (:1677–1830), served-identity extraction (`provider`/`model`/`system_fingerprint` :1281–1286), and
  the capture-hook invocation pattern (:1821–1828). Headers :1064–1068. Timeouts/retry :1507–1676.
- `pathB_capture.py`: `capture_llm_call(*, role, messages, raw_response)` (:191–207),
  `build_response_metadata(raw)` pulls `provider_name`/`model`/`system_fingerprint` (:168–188),
  `llm_role(role)` context manager (:115–124), `is_active()`/`current_llm_role()`.
- sub-PR-4 `role_transport.py`: the `RoleTransport` Protocol `complete(request: RoleRequest) ->
  RoleResponse` (SYNC); `RoleRequest(role, model_slug, messages, params)`; `RoleResponse(raw_text,
  served_model, usage, citations)`. The adapters (`run_mirror/run_sentinel/run_judge`) call
  `transport.complete(request)` synchronously.

## Scope of PR-7/M1 (acceptance criteria)
New module `src/polaris_graph/roles/openai_compatible_transport.py` implementing the sub-PR-4
`RoleTransport` Protocol for the 3 self-hosted verifier roles.

1. `OpenAICompatibleRoleTransport` (implements `RoleTransport`): SYNC `complete(request: RoleRequest)
   -> RoleResponse` that POSTs an OpenAI-compatible `/v1/chat/completions` to a PER-ROLE `base_url`.
   The HTTP client is INJECTED (constructor takes an `httpx.Client` or a transport) so tests pass a
   stub — NO network in tests.
   - **(iter-2 fix, Codex P1) Payload normalization — messages OR prompt.** VERIFIED against the
     adapters: Sentinel sends `request.messages`; Judge + Mirror pass-1 + Mirror pass-2 send
     `request.prompt` (a string). The transport MUST normalize: if `request.messages` is set, use it;
     ELSE build `messages=[{"role":"user","content":request.prompt}]` (prepend a system message if
     `request.params` carries one). The NORMALIZED messages are what get POSTed AND what is passed to
     `capture_llm_call(messages=...)` — so a prompt-only role never sends/captures an empty payload.
   - Pass `request.params` through as TOP-LEVEL request keys (Codex P2): `structured_outputs`/
     `response_format` for Judge, `documents` for Mirror. Reuse the openrouter_client body shape.
   - **(iter-3 fix, Codex P1) Model-VISIBILITY of params on a plain vLLM endpoint.** A plain vLLM
     `/v1/chat/completions` model sees ONLY the `messages` — a top-level `documents` or `pass2_input`
     key is NOT guaranteed model-visible. So during normalization the transport MUST serialize the
     model-relevant params INTO the normalized messages: render `params["documents"]` as an explicit
     evidence context message (each doc_id + text), and render `params["pass2_input"]` (the Mirror
     pass-2 binding: pass-1 answer + `content_hash`) as an explicit message the model must classify.
     Keep them ALSO as top-level keys (for a managed server that consumes them + for test/contract
     introspection), but the messages are the source of truth for what the model reads. Without this,
     live Mirror pass-2 never sees the pass-1 artifact/content_hash and the binding is meaningless.
   - **(iter-4 fix, Codex P1) Citation-OUTPUT contract must be model-visible too.** Mirror pass-1
     sets `params["citations"]=True` — a flag, NOT an output instruction a plain vLLM model obeys.
     When `params["citations"]` is true, the transport MUST render an explicit citation-output
     instruction into the normalized messages: require the answer to cite supported spans in the
     EXACT self-host form `<co>covered text</co:doc_id>` using ONLY the supplied `documents` doc_ids.
     Without this the live model returns plain prose with no `<co>` spans, `parse_cohere_citations`
     finds nothing, `MirrorCitationError` fails closed on EVERY claim, and the whole run holds.
     (Generalizes the rule: for the plain-vLLM convention the transport renders the role's full
     model-visible serving contract — evidence, binding, AND required output format — into `messages`.)
   - Parse the response: `raw_text` = assistant message content; `served_model` = response `model`;
     `usage` = the usage dict.
   - **(iter-2 fix, Codex P1) Cohere `<co>` citation/raw_text invariant.** The transport does NOT
     pre-parse `<co>` spans. For the self-host path it returns `raw_text` AS-IS (tags intact) and
     `citations=None`; `mirror_adapter` parses `<co>` and strips, owning the offset alignment (it
     already handles both the structured-citations and `<co>` paths). NEVER return parsed citations
     alongside un-stripped raw_text — offsets index the TAG-STRIPPED text, so that combination breaks
     the Mirror citation contract. (A future MANAGED transport returning STRUCTURED citation spans
     could fill `RoleResponse.citations` — those are not text-offset; out of scope for M1 self-host.)
2. **Per-role endpoint config** (LAW VI): a resolver `role_endpoint(role) -> (base_url, api_key,
   model_slug)` reading env `PG_<ROLE>_BASE_URL` + `PG_<ROLE>_API_KEY` (fallback OPENROUTER_API_KEY)
   + the lock-sourced model slug. Generator is excluded (not served here).
3. **Capture integration + served ENDPOINT (iter-3 fix, Codex P1):** every `complete()` wraps the
   call in `llm_role(request.role)` and invokes `capture_llm_call(role=request.role,
   messages=normalized_messages, raw_response=raw)` so the Path-B served==pinned gate can later
   verify the live call. served_model is the response `model` (served identity), not the request slug.
   - A self-host vLLM response carries NO `provider_name` and NOT the endpoint it was served from —
     but M4's served==pinned check for a self-host role needs the ENDPOINT. So M1 captures it NOW:
     before calling capture, the transport augments the raw dict with an explicit served block
     `raw["_pathb_served"] = {"endpoint": base_url, "model": served_model}`, and `build_response_metadata`
     in `pathB_capture.py` is extended (small additive, backward-compatible) to surface an optional
     `endpoint` from `_pathb_served` when present. Do NOT fabricate a `provider_name` for vLLM. A test
     asserts the captured record carries the endpoint so M4 can consume it.
4. **Fail LOUD:** an HTTP error / non-200 / malformed body raises a clear `RoleTransportError`
   (never a silent empty RoleResponse that a downstream fail-closed parser would mis-handle). Reuse
   the openrouter_client timeout default (`PG_LLM_TIMEOUT_SECONDS`).
5. **Tests** (`tests/roles/test_openai_compatible_transport.py`), ALL with an injected
   `httpx.MockTransport` (no network): per-role base_url is hit (generator NOT routable here -> raises);
   **(iter-2) a prompt-only request (Judge/Mirror) is normalized to messages AND the SAME normalized
   messages reach capture (assert capture got non-empty messages, not an empty prompt)**; the request
   carries Judge `structured_outputs`/Mirror `documents` when present; response parses to RoleResponse
   (raw_text/served_model/usage); **(iter-3) a Mirror pass-2 request's normalized messages CONTAIN the
   pass-1 `content_hash` (model-visible, not just a params key), and `documents` are rendered into the
   messages; the captured record carries the served `endpoint` (base_url) for M4;** **(iter-4) a
   Mirror pass-1 request (params['citations']=True) normalizes messages containing BOTH the documents
   AND the explicit `<co>covered text</co:doc_id>` citation-output instruction referencing the
   supplied doc_ids;** **(iter-2) a Cohere `<co>` response returns raw_text AS-IS (tags
   intact) with `citations=None` — the transport does NOT pre-parse/strip**; `capture_llm_call` is
   invoked with the right role + served metadata (assert via a registered capture sink); a 500 /
   malformed body raises RoleTransportError.
6. Hygiene: snake_case, explicit imports, named constants, no `except: pass`, no unittest.mock in
   `src/`, no real network anywhere, no `datetime.now()` in library code.

## Files I have ALSO checked / relevant
- `openrouter_client.py` — REUSED patterns (request/response/served-identity/capture); the generator
  stays on its existing async path, NOT routed through this transport. Not modified by M1.
- `pathB_capture.py` — consumed (llm_role + capture_llm_call) + a SMALL ADDITIVE change in this PR:
  `build_response_metadata` surfaces an optional `endpoint` from `_pathb_served` (backward-compatible;
  existing 3-key behavior unchanged when absent). This is the only edit to an existing file.
- sub-PR-4 adapters + role_transport.py Protocol — consumed as-is; this is the concrete impl they
  were designed to accept. The mock transport in tests already proves the adapters; M1 is the real one.
- `role_pipeline.py` RecordingTransport — wraps ANY transport incl. this one; unchanged.

## iter-4 changelog (addresses your iter-3 P1)
- **P1 (Mirror pass-1 `<co>` OUTPUT contract not model-visible):** when `params["citations"]` is
  true, the transport now renders an explicit `<co>covered text</co:doc_id>` citation-output
  instruction (referencing the supplied doc_ids) INTO the normalized messages — so the live model
  is actually told to emit `<co>` spans, not just handed the evidence. Without it every live Mirror
  pass-1 returned plain prose and fail-closed. Tested. See scope item 1.

## iter-3 changelog (addresses your iter-2 P1s; iter-1/P2 retained)
- **P1 (Mirror pass-2 model-visibility):** the transport now SERIALIZES model-relevant params into the
  normalized messages — `documents` rendered as an evidence message, `pass2_input` (pass-1 answer +
  content_hash) rendered as a message the model classifies — because a plain vLLM model sees only
  `messages`. Tested: the pass-2 request's messages contain the content_hash. See scope item 1.
- **P1 (served endpoint for M4):** the transport augments the captured raw with
  `_pathb_served={"endpoint": base_url, "model": served_model}` and `build_response_metadata` is
  extended (small additive) to surface `endpoint`; no fabricated `provider_name`. Tested: captured
  record carries the endpoint. See scope item 3.
- iter-2 retained: prompt→messages normalization (same messages to body AND capture); Cohere `<co>`
  raw_text-as-is + citations=None (mirror_adapter owns parse/strip). iter-1/P2 retained: SYNC new
  module; generator HARD-excluded; top-level keys for response_format/documents/structured_outputs;
  injected MockTransport (no network).

## Questions for Codex (iter-2)
1. Confirm the prompt→messages normalization (same normalized messages to body AND capture) fully
   closes the empty-payload gap for Judge/Mirror.
2. Confirm raw_text-AS-IS + citations=None (mirror_adapter owns `<co>` parse/strip) is the correct
   citation invariant — no offset-misalignment risk remains.
3. Served identity for a self-host vLLM endpoint: served `model` + base_url, NO synthesized
   provider_name — confirm this is what the Path-B served==pinned check (M4) should consume, and that
   M1 should NOT fabricate a provider slug.
4. Any residual correctness/network-in-tests risk.

Hand me APPROVE iff the prompt-normalization, the citation invariant, the served-identity decision,
the injected-no-network-test boundary, and the fail-loud contract are correct.

docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:1:# I-bug-104 — Per-decimal extraction prompt rewrite (FAILED)
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:7:A 100-line rewrite of the generator prompt emphasizing **per-decimal extraction discipline** ("for every numeric value in your sentence, the EXACT digits MUST appear in the cited span — no rounding, no approximation, no near-miss") would reduce strict_verify drops on the `numeric_mismatch` failure mode.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:9:**Reasoning:** the 2026-05-09 audit surfaced sentences like "tirzepatide reduced HbA1c by ~1.5%" cited against a span containing "1.55%" — the 0.05% rounding triggered `numeric_mismatch` drop. A stricter prompt might suppress these near-miss approximations.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:13:- Branch: `bot/I-bug-104-prompt-rewrite` (subsequently abandoned, never PR'd)
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:14:- Modified: `src/polaris_graph/generator/multi_section_generator.py` — replaced ~80-line prompt with 180-line version emphasizing per-decimal discipline + 6 worked examples of "say the same digits or say nothing".
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:30:The over-strict prompt caused the generator to **omit citations** rather than risk a mismatch. Sentences came back without `[#ev:...]` tokens at all — `no_provenance_token` drops shot up from minor to dominant. Net: we traded a small-grain failure (numeric_mismatch on near-miss decimals) for a coarse-grain failure (no provenance at all). Verified output shrank to <40% of baseline.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:32:The prompt's "say nothing if you can't say it exactly" instruction was misread by the generator as "skip the citation if the value is approximate" rather than "use the exact digits from the span".
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:36:The lesson generalizes: **prompt over-discipline can shift failure modes laterally, not reduce them**. Future prompt-engineering attempts on the strict_verify failure-rate problem should A/B compare ALL drop-reason buckets, not just the targeted one.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:38:The 100-line prompt rewrite was reverted on the same day. No production change shipped from this experiment.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:42:- **I-bug-101 (FPR audit):** distinguishes "judge dropped legit sentence" (FPR) from "generator emitted unverifiable sentence" (real generator gap). The right framing for prompt iteration.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:43:- **I-bug-105 + I-bug-108 (already shipped):** two-layer report contract + sentence repair loop. Solved the underlying "don't drop everything just because one sentence fails" problem at the architecture level, not the prompt level.
docs\experiments\i_bug_104_failed.md:44:- **Path A bakeoff (I-bakeoff-A-001):** if a different generator (Qwen 3.5 Plus, Opus 4.7, GPT-5) handles per-decimal discipline natively without prompt over-engineering, the right move is a model swap, not a prompt rewrite.

docs\clinical_rag_validation_sota_2026_05_26.md:31:1. **Prompt-level atom injection.** V4 Pro (DeepSeek's reasoning model) is prompted to emit per-claim `atom_NNN` tokens inline with the generated text, plus `[ev_XXX]` evidence-block citations. The atom catalogue is pre-extracted from corpus markdown tables (per-cell percentages, e.g. `atom_007 = {endpoint: constipation, arm: TZP_15mg, value: 7.1%}`) via `src/polaris_graph/generator/claim_atom_extractor.py`. Approach is "Approach C hybrid" per Codex APPROVE_DESIGN 2026-05-26 — prompt-side instruction plus post-hoc enforcement.
docs\clinical_rag_validation_sota_2026_05_26.md:45:**What it does.** Native API feature (GA Jan 2025) where Claude is provided source documents (PDF / plain text / custom-content blocks) with `citations.enabled=true`, and the response interleaves text blocks with **structured citation blocks containing character-index ranges (0-indexed, exclusive end) for plain text, page numbers for PDFs, or content-block indices for custom content** [^anthropic_citations_docs]. The cited text is verbatim from the source — guaranteed to be a valid pointer because the chunking and citation extraction happen inside Anthropic's pipeline, not via prompt instruction. Customer reports: **source-hallucination + formatting issues 10% → 0%** [^anthropic_citations_blog]. Internal Anthropic evaluations: **+15% recall accuracy over prompt-based custom citation implementations** [^anthropic_citations_blog].
docs\clinical_rag_validation_sota_2026_05_26.md:47:**Latency / cost.** Slight input-token bump (system prompt addition + chunking metadata). Output `cited_text` does NOT count toward output tokens — pure cost saving versus prompt-based "make Claude quote the document" patterns. Compatible with prompt caching (apply `cache_control` to document blocks). Incompatible with structured outputs (`output_config.format`) — they're mutually exclusive.
docs\clinical_rag_validation_sota_2026_05_26.md:137:**What it does.** Use a strong LLM (Claude Opus 4.7, GPT-5, Gemini 2.5 Pro, Llama 3.3 70B) as a judge, prompted to do per-claim faithfulness verification with quoted evidence. Datadog's 2025 engineering blog and Patronus's research both validate this as the highest-quality detection method when no fine-tuned alternative exists [^datadog_judge_2025]. Lynx (§3.3) is the open-source instantiation of this pattern, pre-trained for it.
docs\clinical_rag_validation_sota_2026_05_26.md:143:**Verdict.** **Lynx 8B is the right embodiment** (see §3.3). Don't reinvent the LLM-judge wheel with raw prompts when Lynx exists pre-trained on HaluBench.

docs\clinical_rag_sota_deepest_research_2026_05_27.md:298:Run K generators on the same prompt; extract per-token log-probabilities; compute Shannon entropy per generator + KL divergence between pairs; reduce to statistical moments (mean, variance, skewness, kurtosis, hyperskewness); train stacked classifier (RF + LR + XGB) on these features. docs\process\polaris_master_blueprint_2026_05_28.md:35:Where does the memory plug in? It is a cross-cutting layer wrapped around the locked four models, never a new model inside the line. It reads twice and writes once: it reads trusted priors at Generator time, it reads for cross-time contradictions just before the Judge, and it writes after the Judge. Both reads are signals only. The Judge always decides. The lock that pins the four models pins models and roles, not the words we feed into a prompt, so handing the Generator a memory-derived evidence row is provably not a change to the locked architecture. In the lock file, the memory and the pause layer are declared under a brand-new top-level key that sits beside the four required roles, not inside them, so the freeze gate that counts the four roles never even sees it.
docs\process\polaris_gap_analysis_2026_05_28.md:26:**Gap four — the dev-process loop.** This is the closest to done. The guardrails are committed and working: the architecture lock verifier `scripts/architecture/verify_lock.py`, the weekly drift report `scripts/architecture/weekly_drift_report.py`, the conformance CI gate, the Codex-required CI gate, the runtime lock file, and the freeze guard that ties smokes to the lock. A per-prompt reminder hook also runs and nudges the loop on every prompt. What is missing: the loop is not yet an executable machine. The workflow script the design points to — `.claude/workflows/polaris_task_cycle.js` — does not exist; the whole `.claude/workflows/` folder is absent. The binding rule it claims to live under, a CLAUDE.md section 3.0.1, does not exist either, so the loop is a proposal, not law yet. The reminder hook itself is untracked by git, so it would vanish on a clean checkout. And one more real hole the operator just found: the Codex-required gate is written but is not actually set as a required check on the main branch — branch protection lists no required checks — so the gate exists but is not enforced at merge. The gap is medium. The one main thing to do: write the executable workflow script and add the CLAUDE.md section 3.0.1 rule so the loop becomes binding, and fix the branch-protection setting so the gate is truly enforced.

    4: Mirror role is TWO PASS, each its own transport completion (iter-3 P1-a):
    5:   pass-1: RAG-with-documents (citations on, NO response_format) -> grounded answer + spans
    6:   pass-2: JSON classification (response_format ok, no documents), bound to pass-1 by hash
    7: 
    8: Citation normalization (iter-3 P1-b): pass-1 citations come from `RoleResponse.citations`
    9: when the transport already normalized them (managed path), ELSE from `<co>...</co:doc_ids>`

   11: 
   12: Citation-binding guard (iter-4): every span must point at a `doc_id` actually present in the
   13: supplied `evidence_documents`. A span with an empty doc_id, or citing a doc_id never
   14: provided (hallucinated identity), or MIXING a real cite with a fabricated one, is REJECTED
   15: whole. If NO valid grounded citation survives, raise `MirrorCitationError` (fail closed) —
   16: a non-empty-but-ungrounded citation set must NOT satisfy the binding. Every Mirror claim in
   17: this PR is grounding-required; there is no escape hatch.
   18: 
   19: Binding guard (pass-1<->pass-2): `verify_pass2_binding` MUST hold or `MirrorBindingError` is
   20: raised — an unbound pass-2 is never trusted.

   67: def _strip_co_tags(raw: str) -> str:
   68:     """Strip `<co>...</co:doc_ids>` tags, leaving the covered text, so the cleaned answer
   69:     text's offsets align with the spans `parse_cohere_citations` reports (which index into
   70:     the TAG-STRIPPED text). Replacing each match with its covered group (group 1) mirrors
   71:     exactly how the contract reconstructs cleaned-text offsets.
   72:     """
   73:     return _CO_SPAN_RE.sub(lambda m: m.group(1), raw)
   74:

   76: def _validate_citation_binding(
   77:     spans: list[CitationSpan],
   78:     valid_doc_ids: set[str],
   79: ) -> list[CitationSpan]:
   80:     """Keep only spans whose doc_ids ALL bind to a supplied evidence document.
   81: 
   82:     A span is REJECTED whole if it has no doc_ids (empty/missing) OR if ANY of its doc_ids
   83:     is not in `valid_doc_ids` (a mixed real+hallucinated span is itself a fabrication signal,
   84:     so it does not count as grounding). Returns the surviving grounded spans.
   85:     """

   87:     for span in spans:
   88:         if not span.doc_ids:
   89:             continue  # empty/missing doc_id tuple -> not grounding
   90:         # Reject a span if ANY of its doc_ids is empty/whitespace. An empty doc_id is never
   91:         # grounding, even if the supplied evidence set happens to contain an
   92:         # EvidenceDocument with an empty/whitespace doc_id (Codex diff iter-1 P1: such a
   93:         # doc is excluded from valid_doc_ids, but guard here too — defense in depth).
   94:         if any((not doc_id or not doc_id.strip()) for doc_id in span.doc_ids):
   95:             continue
   96:         if any(doc_id not in valid_doc_ids for doc_id in span.doc_ids):
   97:             continue  # hallucinated (or mixed) identity -> reject whole span
   98:         grounded.append(span)
   99:     return grounded
  100: 
  101: 
  102: def _extract_citations(
  103:     response: RoleResponse,
  104:     valid_doc_ids: set[str],
  105: ) -> list[CitationSpan]:
  106:     """Normalize pass-1 citations from the explicit precedence, then bind-validate them.
  107: 
  108:     Source precedence (iter-3 P1-b): structured `RoleResponse.citations` (managed path) if
  109:     present, ELSE `<co>` spans parsed from `raw_text` (self-host path). Both sources flow
  110:     through the SINGLE `_validate_citation_binding` step (iter-4). Returns ONLY the spans
  111:     that bind to a supplied evidence document.
  112:     """
  113:     if response.citations is not None:
  114:         raw_spans = response.citations
  115:     else:
  116:         raw_spans = parse_cohere_citations(response.raw_text)
  117:     return _validate_citation_binding(raw_spans, valid_doc_ids)
  118: 
  119: 
  120: def build_mirror_pass1_request(
  121:     claim: str,
  122:     evidence_documents: list[EvidenceDocument],
  123:     *,
  124:     model_slug: str,
  125: ) -> RoleRequest:
  126:     """Build the pass-1 RAG-with-documents request (citations on, NO response_format).
  127: 
  128:     Documents ride in `params["documents"]`; `params["citations"] = True` turns on citation
  129:     emission. NO `response_format` — JSON mode is incompatible with documents (F2).
  130:     """
  131:     params = {
  132:         "documents": [
  133:             {"doc_id": doc.doc_id, "text": doc.text} for doc in evidence_documents
  134:         ],
  135:         "citations": True,
  136:     }
  137:     return RoleRequest(
  138:         role=_ROLE,
  139:         model_slug=model_slug,
  140:         prompt=claim,
  141:         params=params,
  142:     )
  143: 
  144: 
  145: def build_mirror_pass2_request(pass1: MirrorPass1, *, model_slug: str) -> RoleRequest:
  146:     """Build the pass-2 JSON-classification request, embedding the pass-1 composite hash.
  147: 
  148:     Uses `build_pass2_input(pass1)` so the request carries the composite `content_hash`
  149:     (answer text + ordered citation bindings). `response_format=json_object` is allowed now
  150:     (no documents in this pass).
  151:     """
  152:     pass2_input = build_pass2_input(pass1)
  153:     params = {
  154:         "response_format": {"type": "json_object"},
  155:         "pass2_input": pass2_input,
  156:     }
  157:     return RoleRequest(
  158:         role=_ROLE,
  159:         model_slug=model_slug,
  160:         prompt="Classify the bound pass-1 artifact and return JSON.",
  161:         params=params,
  162:     )
  163: 
  164: 
  165: def _parse_pass2(raw_text: str) -> MirrorPass2:
  166:     """Parse a pass-2 transport response into MirrorPass2.
  167: 
  168:     The classification JSON must carry the `content_hash` (the binding) and a
  169:     `classification`; an optional `rationale` is preserved. JSON decode / shape errors
  170:     propagate (fail loud) rather than fabricate a verdict.
  171:     """
  172:     payload = json.loads(raw_text)
  173:     return MirrorPass2(
  174:         content_hash=payload[_CONTENT_HASH_KEY],
  175:         classification=payload[_CLASSIFICATION_KEY],
  176:         rationale=payload.get(_RATIONALE_KEY),
  177:     )
  178: 
  179: 
  180: def run_mirror(
  181:     transport: RoleTransport,
  182:     claim: str,
  183:     evidence_documents: list[EvidenceDocument],
  184:     *,
  185:     model_slug: str,
  186: ) -> tuple[MirrorPass2, list[RoleCallRecord]]:
  187:     """Run the two Mirror passes and return MirrorPass2 + a 2-element RoleCallRecord list.
  188: 
  189:     Pass-1: RAG-with-documents; normalize + bind-validate citations (iter-4). If no grounded
  190:     citation survives, raise `MirrorCitationError` (fail closed). Pass-2: JSON classification
  191:     bound by hash; if `verify_pass2_binding` is False, raise `MirrorBindingError` (fail
  192:     closed). BOTH completions get their own RoleCallRecord (iter-3 P1-a) so the Path-B gate
  193:     can verify served==pinned per call.
  194:     """
  195:     # Build the citation-identity pool from supplied documents, EXCLUDING any empty/whitespace
  196:     # doc_id so a citation with an empty doc_id can never bind (Codex diff iter-1 P1).
  197:     valid_doc_ids = {
  198:         doc.doc_id for doc in evidence_documents if doc.doc_id and doc.doc_id.strip()
  199:     }
  200: 
  201:     # --- pass 1: RAG with documents + citations -------------------------------------
  202:     pass1_request = build_mirror_pass1_request(
  203:         claim, evidence_documents, model_slug=model_slug
  204:     )
  205:     pass1_response: RoleResponse = transport.complete(pass1_request)
  206: 
  207:     grounded_spans = _extract_citations(pass1_response, valid_doc_ids)
  208:     if not grounded_spans:
  209:         # Fail closed: no citation binds to a supplied document for this grounding-required
  210:         # claim. A non-empty-but-ungrounded citation set lands here too (it was rejected).
  211:         raise MirrorCitationError(
  212:             "Mirror pass-1 produced no citation grounded in the supplied evidence documents "
  213:             f"(claim={claim!r}); refusing to treat as grounded."
  214:         )
  215: 
  216:     # On the self-host path, store the TAG-STRIPPED answer so the span offsets (which index
  217:     # the cleaned text) align with the stored answer_text.
  218:     if pass1_response.citations is not None:
  219:         answer_text = pass1_response.raw_text
  220:     else:
  221:         answer_text = _strip_co_tags(pass1_response.raw_text)
  222:     pass1 = MirrorPass1(answer_text=answer_text, citation_spans=grounded_spans)
  223: 
  224:     pass1_record = RoleCallRecord(
  225:         role=_ROLE,
  226:         model_slug=model_slug,
  227:         served_model=pass1_response.served_model,
  228:         raw_text=pass1_response.raw_text,
  229:         parsed=pass1,
  230:     )
  231: 
  232:     # --- pass 2: JSON classification bound to pass-1 --------------------------------
  233:     pass2_request = build_mirror_pass2_request(pass1, model_slug=model_slug)
  234:     pass2_response: RoleResponse = transport.complete(pass2_request)
  235:     pass2 = _parse_pass2(pass2_response.raw_text)
  236: 
  237:     pass2_record = RoleCallRecord(
  238:         role=_ROLE,
  239:         model_slug=model_slug,
  240:         served_model=pass2_response.served_model,
  241:         raw_text=pass2_response.raw_text,
  242:         parsed=pass2,
  243:     )
  244: 
  245:     if not verify_pass2_binding(pass1, pass2):
  246:         # Fail closed: pass-2 classified a different (answer+citations) artifact than pass-1.
  247:         raise MirrorBindingError(
  248:             "Mirror pass-2 content_hash does not bind to the pass-1 artifact; "
  249:             "refusing to trust an unbound classification."
  250:         )
  251: 
  252:     return pass2, [pass1_record, pass2_record]

   14: Served-identity provenance: ``build_response_metadata`` reads ONLY genuinely-served fields
   15: from the provider response (OpenRouter ``provider`` / served ``model`` / ``system_fingerprint``)
   16: and DROPS missing fields. Request-derived values are never substituted, so a response that
   17: fails to report its served provider/model makes the gate fail loud (in ``assert_post_run``)
   18: rather than silently pass on request-derived data.
   19: """
   20: 
   21: from __future__ import annotations
   22: 
   23: import contextlib
   24: import contextvars
   25: import hashlib
   26: import json
   27: import logging
   28: from typing import Iterator
   29: 
   30: logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
   31: 
   32: # Run-scoped collectors. The contextvars hold REFERENCES to a shared list/set; capture
   33: # mutates them in place so appends inside asyncio child tasks (which copy the context by
   34: # reference) remain visible at the top level where the runner reads them.
   35: _SINK: contextvars.ContextVar[list | None] = contextvars.ContextVar("_PATHB_SINK", default=None)
   36: _ROLE: contextvars.ContextVar[str | None] = contextvars.ContextVar("_PATHB_ROLE", default=None)
   37: _RETRIEVAL: contextvars.ContextVar[set | None] = contextvars.ContextVar("_PATHB_RETRIEVAL", default=None)
   38: # I-bug-946 (#932): per-role resolved provider (e.g. {"generator":"Fireworks","evaluator":"Novita"}).
   39: # Populated by gate_around_question() after preflight resolves each role's actual served provider
   40: # via GET /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints. openrouter_client and entailment_judge read this to force
   41: # singleton provider routing in their request bodies (otherwise OpenRouter's silent fallback would
   42: # defeat the strict-identity guarantee that smoke #15 caught: evaluator routed to Novita while pin
   43: # expected Fireworks). Per Codex iter-2 P2: ContextVar lives in src (NOT scripts/) so the hot path
   44: # never imports scripts. Codex APPROVE iter 2 on I-bug-946 brief.
   45: _ROLE_PROVIDER: contextvars.ContextVar[dict | None] = contextvars.ContextVar(
   46:     "_PATHB_ROLE_PROVIDER", default=None,
   47: )
   48: 
   49: 
   50: def register_pathB_capture() -> None:
   51:     """Begin capture for the current run (fresh collectors). Call once at run start."""
   52:     _SINK.set([])
   53:     _RETRIEVAL.set(set())
   54: 
   55: 
   56: def clear_pathB_capture() -> None:
   57:     """End capture (gate off again). Call at run end."""
   58:     _SINK.set(None)
   59:     _ROLE.set(None)
   60:     _RETRIEVAL.set(None)
   61:     _ROLE_PROVIDER.set(None)
   62: 
   63: 
   64: def set_role_providers(mapping: dict[str, str]):
   65:     """I-bug-946 (#932): set the resolved per-role provider mapping for the gate run.
   66: 
   67:     Called by gate_around_question() AFTER preflight() resolves each role's served provider
   68:     via OpenRouter's /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints. Returns a token; pair with
   69:     reset_role_providers() in try/finally so the mapping never leaks beyond the gate scope.
   70:     """
   71:     return _ROLE_PROVIDER.set(mapping)
   72: 
   73: 
   74: def reset_role_providers(token) -> None:
   75:     _ROLE_PROVIDER.reset(token)
   76: 
   77: 
   78: def current_role_provider() -> str | None:
   79:     """Return the resolved provider for the CURRENT role (read via _ROLE contextvar).
   80: 
   81:     Returns None if either the gate is off (mapping is None) or the current role has no
   82:     entry in the mapping. openrouter_client calls this; when None it falls back to its
   83:     current env-driven path (gate-off mode).
   84: 
   85:     NOTE: entailment_judge must NOT use this — see get_role_provider() below.
   86:     """
   87:     mapping = _ROLE_PROVIDER.get()
   88:     if mapping is None:
   89:         return None
   90:     role = _ROLE.get()
   91:     if role is None:
   92:         return None
   93:     return mapping.get(role)
   94: 
   95: 
   96: def get_role_provider(role: str) -> str | None:
   97:     """Explicit-role lookup, NOT keyed off the ambient _ROLE contextvar.
   98: 
   99:     I-bug-946 (#932) Codex iter-1 diff P1#2: the entailment judge posts the evaluator
  100:     model but is INVOKED from within the generator's _ROLE scope (provenance verification
  101:     fires during section generation). Using current_role_provider() would resolve to the
  102:     generator's provider (Fireworks) for a Gemma post — Fireworks doesn't host Gemma →
  103:     silent re-route. The judge must pass role="evaluator" explicitly.
  104:     """
  105:     mapping = _ROLE_PROVIDER.get()
  106:     if mapping is None:
  107:         return None
  108:     return mapping.get(role)
  109: 
  110: 
  111: def is_active() -> bool:

  113: 
  114: 
  115: @contextlib.contextmanager
  116: def llm_role(role: str) -> Iterator[None]:
  117:     """Scope the role tag for LLM calls made inside the block (token set + restore).
  118: 
  119:     Use a context manager (not a sticky setter) so a role never leaks to later calls."""
  120:     token = _ROLE.set(role)
  121:     try:
  122:         yield
  123:     finally:
  124:         _ROLE.reset(token)
  125:

  128:     """Set the role tag and return a token to restore on. Pair with reset_role(token)
  129:     inside a try/finally — equivalent guarantee to llm_role() ctx-mgr, used where
  130:     re-indenting a large multi-line call block under `with` would be invasive."""
  131:     return _ROLE.set(role)
  132: 
  133: 
  134: def reset_role(token) -> None:
  135:     _ROLE.reset(token)
  136: 
  137: 
  138: def current_llm_role() -> str | None:
  139:     return _ROLE.get()
  140: 
  141: 
  142: def record_retrieval_attempt(backend: str) -> None:
  143:     """Record that a required retrieval backend ('serper'|'semantic_scholar') was attempted."""
  144:     backends = _RETRIEVAL.get()
  145:     if backends is not None:
  146:         backends.add(backend)
  147: 
  148:

  150:     backends = _RETRIEVAL.get()

  152: 
  153: 
  154: def collected_calls() -> list[dict]:
  155:     sink = _SINK.get()
  156:     return list(sink) if sink is not None else []
  157: 
  158: 
  159: def request_hash(messages) -> str:
  160:     """Stable hash of the prompt messages (presence/integrity, not content storage)."""
  161:     try:
  162:         payload = json.dumps(messages, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
  163:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
  164:         payload = repr(messages)
  165:     return hashlib.sha256(payload.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
  166: 
  167: 
  168: def build_response_metadata(raw_response: dict | None) -> dict:
  169:     """Served-identity metadata from the provider response — PROVEN-present fields only.
  170: 
  171:     provider_name <- raw['provider'] (OpenRouter), model <- served raw['model'],
  172:     system_fingerprint <- raw['system_fingerprint']. None/missing fields are DROPPED
  173:     (never request-filled), so an unreported served provider/model surfaces as a gate
  174:     failure rather than a false pass.
  175: 
  176:     Streaming responses synthesize ``data`` with a request-derived ``model`` fallback, so
  177:     the client stashes the genuinely-SSE-served identity under ``_pathb_served``; when that
  178:     key is present it is the authoritative source (request-derived ``data['model']`` is
  179:     never counted as served)."""
  180:     raw = raw_response or {}
  181:     served = raw.get("_pathb_served")
  182:     src = served if isinstance(served, dict) else raw
  183:     meta = {
  184:         "provider_name": src.get("provider"),
  185:         "model": src.get("model"),
  186:         "system_fingerprint": src.get("system_fingerprint"),
  187:     }
  188:     return {k: v for k, v in meta.items() if v is not None}
  189: 
  190: 
  191: def capture_llm_call(*, role: str, messages, raw_response: dict | None) -> None:
  192:     """Best-effort: append one captured provider completion. Never raises; no-op when off."""
  193:     sink = _SINK.get()
  194:     if sink is None:
  195:         return
  196:     try:
  197:         sink.append(
  198:             {
  199:                 "call_id": f"{role}-{len(sink)}",
  200:                 "role": role,
  201:                 "prompt_messages_present": bool(messages),
  202:                 "request_hash": request_hash(messages),
  203:                 "response_metadata": build_response_metadata(raw_response),
  204:             }
  205:         )
  206:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture must never break generation
  207:         logger.warning("[pathB] capture_llm_call failed (%s) — call not recorded", exc)

 1769:         # empty content at their own level with retry + extraction.

 1772:         # silently returning empty strings that cascade into downstream failures.

 1776:                 "reasoning_content for %s (model=%s, %d input tokens)",

 1778:                 data.get("model", self.model),
 1779:                 input_tokens,
 1780:             )
 1781:             raise ValueError(
 1782:                 f"LLM returned no usable content for {call_type} "
 1783:                 f"(model={data.get('model', '?')}, input_tokens={input_tokens})"
 1784:             )

 1786:         if not content and reasoning:
 1787:             logger.warning(
 1788:                 "[polaris graph] COT-1: Content empty for %s, reasoning has "
 1789:                 "%d chars (reasoning_enabled=%s, response_format=%s). "
 1790:                 "Returning as-is — caller handles recovery.",
 1791:                 call_type,
 1792:                 len(reasoning),
 1793:                 reasoning_enabled,
 1794:                 bool(response_format),
 1795:             )

 1802:             reasoning_tokens=reasoning_tokens,
 1803:             model=data.get("model", self.model),
 1804:             duration_ms=duration_ms,
 1805:             raw_response=data,
 1806:         )
 1807: 
 1808:         # I-gen-004 (#496): capture the raw completed provider response to the
 1809:         # run-scoped reasoning-trace sink BEFORE any caller-level promotion /
 1810:         # </think> extraction / retry / ReasoningFirstTruncationError raise.
 1811:         _capture_reasoning_trace(result, content, reasoning)

   50:     extra = "|".join(re.escape(n) for n in _EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
   51:     pat = re.compile(
   52:         rf"os\.(?:getenv|environ\.get)\(\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+|{extra})['\"]"
   53:         rf"|os\.environ\[\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+|{extra})['\"]"
   54:     )
   55:     out: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
   56:     for root in roots:
   57:         for py in root.rglob("*.py"):
   58:             try:
   59:                 lines = py.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore").splitlines()
   60:             except OSError:
   61:                 continue
   62:             for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
   63:                 for m in pat.finditer(line):
   64:                     name = m.group(1) or m.group(2)
   65:                     out.setdefault(name, set()).add(f"{py.as_posix()}:{i}")
   66:     return {k: sorted(v) for k, v in out.items()}
   67: 
   68: # Volatile response fields EXCLUDED from the served-identity surrogate (Codex iter-5 P2).
   69: _VOLATILE_METADATA_FIELDS = frozenset(
   70:     {"id", "request_id", "created", "timestamp", "usage", "prompt_tokens",
   71:      "completion_tokens", "total_tokens", "latency", "latency_ms", "cost", "x-request-id"}
   72: )
   73: 
   74: 
   75: class GateError(RuntimeError):
   76:     """Fatal gate violation — the run is INVALID and must be discarded, never scored."""
   77: 
   78: 
   79: def is_secret_var(name: str) -> bool:
   80:     """True iff `name` is a credential whose VALUE must be redacted (not a *_TOKENS knob)."""
   81:     if name in _SECRET_EXPLICIT:
   82:         return True
   83:     if name.endswith(("_MAX_TOKENS", "_TOKENS", "_TOKEN_BUDGET")):
   84:         return False
   85:     return name.endswith(_SECRET_SUFFIXES)
   86: 
   87: 
   88: def enumerate_control_surface(roots: list[Path]) -> list[str]:
   89:     """Scan source for every PG_*/OPENROUTER_* env var actually read (Codex: complete set).
   90: 
   91:     Greps os.getenv / os.environ.get / os.environ[...] reads — NOT a handpicked list.
   92:     """
   93:     pat = re.compile(
   94:         r"os\.(?:getenv|environ\.get)\(\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+)['\"]"
   95:         r"|os\.environ\[\s*['\"]((?:PG_|OPENROUTER_)[A-Z0-9_]+)['\"]"
   96:     )
   97:     found: set[str] = set()
   98:     for root in roots:
   99:         for py in root.rglob("*.py"):
  100:             try:
  101:                 text = py.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
  102:             except OSError:
  103:                 continue
  104:             for m in pat.finditer(text):
  105:                 found.add(m.group(1) or m.group(2))
  106:     return sorted(found)
  107: 
  108: 
  109: def _redact(name: str, value: str | None, salt: bytes) -> dict:
  110:     """Secret presence record: present/length/salted-HMAC only — never the value (Codex P1)."""
  111:     if value is None:
  112:         return {"present": False, "length": 0, "salted_hmac": None}
  113:     digest = hmac.new(salt, value.encode("utf-8"), hashlib.sha256).hexdigest()
  114:     return {"present": True, "length": len(value), "salted_hmac": digest}
  115: 
  116: 
  117: def build_effective_config(control_vars: list[str], salt: bytes) -> dict:
  118:     """Snapshot the full control surface; secret VALUES redacted (Codex P1)."""
  119:     cfg: dict[str, dict] = {}
  120:     for name in control_vars:
  121:         val = os.environ.get(name)
  122:         if is_secret_var(name):
  123:             cfg[name] = {"secret": True, **_redact(name, val, salt)}
  124:         else:
  125:             cfg[name] = {"secret": False, "value": val, "set": val is not None}
  126:     return cfg
  127: 
  128: 
  129: def effective_config_hash(cfg: dict) -> str:
  130:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(cfg, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
  131: 
  132: 
  133: def served_identity(call_metadata: dict) -> str:
  134:     """Stable per-role served-identity surrogate (Codex iter-4 P1 + iter-5 P2).
  135: 
  136:     OpenRouter has no stable `model_version`; use provider_name + model + system_fingerprint
  137:     (+ any stable router metadata), EXCLUDING volatile fields. Missing the agreed surrogate
  138:     fields is caught by the caller (fatal), not silently hashed to a constant here.
  139:     """
  140:     stable = {
  141:         k: v for k, v in call_metadata.items()
  142:         if k not in _VOLATILE_METADATA_FIELDS
  143:     }
  144:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(stable, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
  145: 
  146: 
  147: @dataclass
  148: class RolePin:
  149:     role: str            # "generator" | "evaluator"
  150:     model_slug: str      # FULL OpenRouter slug, e.g. "deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro" — EXACT match
  151:     provider_name: str
  152:     surrogate_fields: tuple[str, ...]   # the metadata fields PROVEN present at preflight
  153:     canonical_slug: str | None = None   # I-bug-945 (#931): OpenRouter dated snapshot resolved
  154:     # at preflight via GET /api/v1/models. The alias `model_slug` is the env-pin handle; the
  155:     # canonical_slug (e.g. deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro-20260423) is what gets served as `model`
  156:     # in chat completions and is the actual pre-registration anchor in pathB_gate_pin.json.
  157:     # Trailing defaulted field per Codex P2#3 (don't break positional RolePin call sites).
  158: 
  159: 
  160: def _role_surrogate(metadata: dict, surrogate_fields: tuple[str, ...] | list) -> str:
  161:     """The served-identity surrogate over the PINNED fields only (Codex P1 — exact pin)."""
  162:     picked = {f: metadata.get(f) for f in surrogate_fields}
  163:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(picked, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
  164: 
  165: 
  166: def preflight(
  167:     control_vars: list[str],
  168:     role_pins: list[RolePin],
  169:     salt: bytes,
  170:     reachability_prober=None,
  171:     source_map: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,
  172:     roots: list[Path] | None = None,
  173:     offline: bool = False,
  174:     enforce_architecture_coverage: bool = True,
  175: ) -> dict:
  176:     """Fatal preflight. Returns the pin record to hash-pin BEFORE the run.
  177: 
  178:     The gate FORCES the complete control surface (Codex iter-2 P1): it always unions the
  179:     retrieval/credential env into `control_vars`, and if `roots` is given it also unions the
  180:     grepped PG_*/OPENROUTER_* surface — so a caller passing `[]` cannot produce an empty config.
  181: 
  182:     Reachability is enforce-by-default for real runs (Codex iter-2 P1): if `offline` is False
  183:     and no prober is given, `real_retrieval_prober` is used (live ping). Tests pass
  184:     `offline=True` to skip the network. `reachability_checked=False` is therefore only
  185:     possible in an explicitly-offline (test) run, never a real run gate.
  186:     """
  187:     # FORCE the complete control surface (retrieval creds always; grepped surface if roots given)
  188:     surface = set(control_vars or [])
  189:     if roots:
  190:         surface |= set(full_control_surface(roots))
  191:     surface |= set(_EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
  192:     control_vars = sorted(surface)
  193:     # reachability: enforce-by-default for real runs
  194:     if not offline and reachability_prober is None:
  195:         reachability_prober = real_retrieval_prober
  196:     # 1. fallbacks OFF
  197:     if os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS", "true").strip().lower() not in ("false", "0", "no"):
  198:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS must be false (it defaults TRUE)")
  199:     # 2. provider routing — per-role resolution at preflight (I-bug-946 #932).
  200:     # The env supplies a candidate list (comma-separated). Each role's actual served provider
  201:     # is resolved via OpenRouter's per-model endpoints endpoint and pinned per role. The old
  202:     # "singleton" check rejected multi-provider orders, but disjoint model provider sets
  203:     # require a multi-entry order (e.g. fireworks for deepseek-v4-pro, novita for gemma).
  204:     order = (os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER") or "").strip()
  205:     provider_order_list = [p.strip() for p in order.split(",") if p.strip()]
  206:     if not provider_order_list:
  207:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER must list at least one candidate provider")
  208:     # 3. required retrieval capability — PRESENCE *and* REACHABILITY (Codex P1)
  209:     missing = [c for c in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS if not os.environ.get(c)]
  210:     if missing:
  211:         raise GateError(f"required retrieval credentials absent — not full-power: {missing}")
  212:     if reachability_prober is not None:
  213:         for cred, backend in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS_TO_BACKENDS.items():
  214:             if not reachability_prober(backend):
  215:                 raise GateError(f"retrieval backend {backend!r} unreachable/invalid-key — not full-power")
  216:     # 4. each role pin must declare which surrogate fields it PROVED present + a full slug
  217:     for rp in role_pins:
  218:         if not rp.surrogate_fields:
  219:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: no served-identity surrogate fields proven present")
  220:         if "/" not in rp.model_slug:
  221:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: model_slug must be the FULL slug (provider/model), got {rp.model_slug!r}")
  222:         # I-bug-945 (#931): resolve OpenRouter alias to its dated canonical_slug at preflight.
  223:         # The catalog is the single source of truth; fail closed if the alias is unknown.
  224:         # Skipped on offline runs (unit tests pass canonical_slug directly when needed).
  225:         if not offline and rp.canonical_slug is None:
  226:             rp.canonical_slug = resolve_canonical_slug(rp.model_slug)
  227:         # I-bug-946 (#932): resolve per-role provider via /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints.
  228:         # Codex iter-1 diff P1: online preflight MUST always overwrite provider_name from
  229:         # the resolver, because _role_pins() previously pre-seeded provider_name from the
  230:         # env's first entry (now changed to empty, but the always-overwrite invariant is
  231:         # the defense-in-depth — any future caller passing a non-empty provider_name still
  232:         # gets re-resolved at preflight, so the persisted pin reflects the actual resolution).
  233:         # Offline tests skip the resolver; if provider_name is empty under offline, fall
  234:         # back to the env's first entry (test-compat — tests still drive the pipeline via
  235:         # OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER and expect the served provider to match the pin).
  236:         if not offline:
  237:             rp.provider_name = resolve_role_provider(rp.model_slug, provider_order_list)
  238:         elif not rp.provider_name and provider_order_list:
  239:             rp.provider_name = provider_order_list[0]
  240:     # I-bug-946 (Codex iter 2 P2#3 + iter-1 diff P2#2): enforce that the effective
  241:     # entailment model equals the effective evaluator model. Compare EFFECTIVE values
  242:     # (with their defaults) so a single env override that diverges from the default still
  243:     # fails closed — not only the "both env vars set divergently" case.
  244:     _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL = "google/gemma-4-31b-it"  # mirror entailment_judge.py:79
  245:     _DEFAULT_EVALUATOR_MODEL = "google/gemma-4-31b-it"   # mirror pathB_runner.py:37
  246:     eff_entail = (os.environ.get("PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL") or _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL).strip()
  247:     eff_eval = (os.environ.get("PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL") or _DEFAULT_EVALUATOR_MODEL).strip()
  248:     if eff_entail != eff_eval:
  249:         raise GateError(
  250:             f"effective PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL={eff_entail!r} != effective PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL"
  251:             f"={eff_eval!r}; the gate cannot pin two different evaluator-family models"
  252:         )
  253:     # I-meta-001 (#933) Step 9: enforce architecture coverage at preflight.
  254:     # If config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml exists, its required_roles set
  255:     # MUST match the role_pins set (every locked role pinned). Gate refuses if missing.
  256:     # offline=True implies test mode (unit fixtures intentionally use 2-role pins);
  257:     # tests can also explicitly opt out via enforce_architecture_coverage=False.
  258:     _enforce_coverage = enforce_architecture_coverage and not offline
  259:     arch_coverage = (
  260:         _assert_architecture_coverage(role_pins) if _enforce_coverage
  261:         else {"status": "skipped", "missing_roles": [], "lock_status": None,
  262:               "warning": "architecture coverage check skipped (offline=True or enforce=False)"}
  263:     )
  264:     cfg = build_effective_config(control_vars, salt)
  265:     return {
  266:         "effective_config": cfg,
  267:         "effective_config_hash": effective_config_hash(cfg),
  268:         "control_vars": control_vars,             # the RESOLVED surface (post-run rebuilds from this)
  269:         "control_source_map": source_map or {},   # name -> [file:line, ...] provenance (Codex P2)
  270:         "role_pins": [vars(rp) | {"surrogate_fields": list(rp.surrogate_fields)} for rp in role_pins],
  271:         "architecture_coverage": arch_coverage,  # I-meta-001 Step 9
  272:         "reachability_checked": reachability_prober is not None,
  273:         "openrouter_allow_fallbacks": False,
  274:         "openrouter_provider_order": order,
  275:     }
  276: 
  277: 
  278: def _assert_architecture_coverage(role_pins: list) -> dict:
  279:     """I-meta-001 (#933) Step 9: refuse the smoke unless every locked architecture role
  280:     is present in role_pins.
  281: 
  282:     Loads ``config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml``. If the lock exists AND
  283:     its status is ``locked``, every ``required_roles`` key must appear in role_pins.
  284:     If status is ``codex_approved_pending_operator_signature`` (the explicit operator
  285:     freeze state), the gate refuses ALL smokes — smokes resume only after the lock is
  286:     promoted to ``locked`` via scripts/architecture/verify_lock.py.
  287: 
  288:     When the lock file is missing (legacy path / pre-Step-4 commits), behavior is
  289:     permissive: accept any role_pins shape but emit a warning in the returned dict.
  290: 
  291:     Returns a dict {"status": ..., "missing_roles": [...], "lock_status": ...}.
  292:     Raises GateError when coverage is enforced and violated.
  293:     """
  294:     from pathlib import Path
  295:     lock_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "config" / "architecture" / "polaris_runtime_lock.yaml"
  296:     if not lock_path.exists():
  297:         return {"status": "no_lock", "missing_roles": [], "lock_status": None,
  298:                 "warning": "no config/architecture/polaris_runtime_lock.yaml — coverage not enforced"}
  299: 
  300:     try:
  301:         import yaml  # type: ignore[import-not-found]
  302:         lock = yaml.safe_load(lock_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  303:     except Exception as exc:
  304:         raise GateError(f"architecture lock unreadable: {exc}") from exc
  305: 
  306:     lock_status = lock.get("status")
  307:     required_roles = set(lock.get("required_roles", {}).keys())
  308:     pinned_roles = {rp.role for rp in role_pins}
  309:     missing = required_roles - pinned_roles
  310: 
  311:     if lock_status == "codex_approved_pending_operator_signature":
  312:         raise GateError(
  313:             "architecture lock status is 'codex_approved_pending_operator_signature' — "
  314:             "smokes FROZEN per operator directive (I-meta-001 #933). Promote the lock to "
  315:             "status: locked via scripts/architecture/verify_lock.py after all propagation "
  316:             "checkpoints are complete + tests pass + operator commits."
  317:         )
  318: 
  319:     if lock_status == "locked" and missing:
  320:         raise GateError(
  321:             f"architecture coverage incomplete: locked roles {required_roles!r} "
  322:             f"but pinned only {pinned_roles!r}; missing {missing!r}. The 4-role "
  323:             f"architecture requires generator + mirror + sentinel + judge."
  324:         )
  325: 
  326:     return {
  327:         "status": "ok" if not missing else "partial",
  328:         "missing_roles": sorted(missing),
  329:         "lock_status": lock_status,
  330:         "required_roles": sorted(required_roles),
  331:         "pinned_roles": sorted(pinned_roles),
  332:     }
  333: 
  334: 
  335: def resolve_role_provider(model_slug: str, provider_order: list[str]) -> str:
  336:     """I-bug-946 (#932): resolve a role's served provider at preflight.
  337: 
  338:     OpenRouter's GET /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints returns the providers that actually serve
  339:     a model. Smoke #15 demonstrated that without per-role resolution, OpenRouter silently
  340:     routes a role to a provider OUTSIDE the env-pinned order (gemma is not on Fireworks, so
  341:     the evaluator was routed to Novita despite `OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER=fireworks` +
  342:     `allow_fallbacks=false`). The gate caught it correctly; the pin model was wrong.
  343: 
  344:     Algorithm:
  345:       1. Fetch /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints; parse `data.endpoints`.
  346:       2. Eligible = endpoints with status absent OR status==0. status != 0 means degraded /
  347:          lower-priority per OpenRouter docs (Codex iter-2 P2#4).
  348:       3. Intersect eligible providers (case-insensitive) with `provider_order`.
  349:       4. Return the catalog-cased provider_name of the FIRST match in `provider_order`.
  350:       5. Fail closed with diagnostic if no match OR endpoints list is empty.
  351: 
  352:     Codex APPROVE iter 2 on choice C, brief at .codex/I-bug-946/brief_iter2.md.
  353:     """
  354:     import requests
  355:     api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
  356:     headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
  357:     url = f"https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models/{model_slug}/endpoints"
  358:     try:
  359:         r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
  360:         r.raise_for_status()
  361:         endpoints = r.json().get("data", {}).get("endpoints", [])
  362:     except Exception as exc:
  363:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter endpoints catalog unreachable for {model_slug!r}: {exc}") from exc
  364:     if not endpoints:
  365:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter has no endpoints for model {model_slug!r} (model offline?)")
  366:     eligible: list[str] = []
  367:     for ep in endpoints:
  368:         status = ep.get("status")
  369:         if status is None or status == 0:
  370:             name = ep.get("provider_name")
  371:             if name:
  372:                 eligible.append(name)
  373:     if not eligible:
  374:         raise GateError(
  375:             f"OpenRouter has no eligible (status==0) endpoints for {model_slug!r}; "
  376:             f"all endpoints degraded"
  377:         )
  378:     eligible_lower = {n.lower(): n for n in eligible}  # case-insensitive lookup, catalog cased value
  379:     for wanted in provider_order:
  380:         catalog_cased = eligible_lower.get(wanted.strip().lower())
  381:         if catalog_cased is not None:
  382:             return catalog_cased
  383:     raise GateError(
  384:         f"OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER={provider_order!r} has no intersection with eligible "
  385:         f"endpoints for {model_slug!r}; available: {sorted(set(eligible))}"
  386:     )
  387: 
  388: 
  389: def resolve_canonical_slug(model_slug: str) -> str | None:
  390:     """I-bug-945 (#931): Resolve OpenRouter alias to its dated canonical_slug at preflight.
  391: 
  392:     OpenRouter exposes a list at GET /api/v1/models with `id` (alias) + `canonical_slug`
  393:     (dated snapshot) per entry. The chat-completions response returns `model=<canonical_slug>`
  394:     while the env pin uses `<id>`. Resolving at preflight lets `assert_post_run` accept the
  395:     served canonical_slug without losing pre-registration integrity — the resolved value is
  396:     persisted in `pathB_gate_pin.json` and becomes the audit anchor.
  397: 
  398:     Returns the canonical_slug, or None if it equals model_slug (no dated suffix exposed).
  399:     Raises GateError if the slug is not in the catalog (fail closed) — Codex P2#2.
  400:     """
  401:     import requests
  402:     api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
  403:     headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
  404:     try:
  405:         r = requests.get("https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models", headers=headers, timeout=20)
  406:         r.raise_for_status()
  407:         data = r.json().get("data", [])
  408:     except Exception as exc:
  409:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter models catalog unreachable: {exc}") from exc
  410:     for m in data:
  411:         if m.get("id") == model_slug:
  412:             cs = m.get("canonical_slug")
  413:             return cs if cs and cs != model_slug else None
  414:     raise GateError(f"OpenRouter catalog has no entry for pinned slug {model_slug!r} (alias unknown)")
  415: 
  416: 
  417: def real_retrieval_prober(backend: str) -> bool:
  418:     """Minimal live reachability ping per backend (Codex P1). Returns True iff a valid
  419:     response. Cheap; runs once at preflight. Imported lazily to keep the module light."""
  420:     import requests
  421:     try:
  422:         if backend == "serper":
  423:             r = requests.post(
  424:                 "https://google.serper.dev/search",
  425:                 headers={"X-API-KEY": os.environ["SERPER_API_KEY"], "Content-Type": "application/json"},
  426:                 json={"q": "metformin"}, timeout=15,
  427:             )
  428:             return r.status_code == 200
  429:         if backend == "semantic_scholar":
  430:             r = requests.get(
  431:                 "https://api.semanticscholar.org/graph/v1/paper/search",
  432:                 headers={"x-api-key": os.environ["SEMANTIC_SCHOLAR_API_KEY"]},
  433:                 params={"query": "metformin", "limit": 1}, timeout=20,
  434:             )
  435:             return r.status_code == 200
  436:     except Exception:
  437:         return False
  438:     return False

   35: class MockTransport:
   36:     """Configurable mock `RoleTransport` keyed on the request role + Mirror pass.
   37: 
   38:     - Mirror pass-1 (no `pass2_input` in params): returns a managed-path grounded citation
   39:       span pointing at `doc1` (in the evidence), so `_extract_citations` yields a grounded span
   40:       and the Mirror does NOT fail closed. `mirror_fail_closed=True` flips pass-1 to an
   41:       ungrounded citation (doc_id not in evidence) so `run_mirror` raises MirrorCitationError.
   42:     - Mirror pass-2 (`pass2_input` present): echoes the embedded `content_hash` back in JSON so
   43:       `verify_pass2_binding` holds.
   44:     - Sentinel: returns `<score>yes</score>` (UNGROUNDED) or `<score>no</score>` (GROUNDED).
   45:     - Judge: returns the configured verdict token.
   46: 
   47:     `seen_roles` records the ordered role sequence so tests can assert Mirror -> Sentinel ->
   48:     Judge ordering.
   49:     """
   50: 
   51:     def __init__(
   52:         self,
   53:         *,
   54:         sentinel_grounded: bool = True,
   55:         judge_verdict: str = "VERIFIED",
   56:         mirror_fail_closed: bool = False,
   57:     ) -> None:
   58:         self._sentinel_grounded = sentinel_grounded
   59:         self._judge_verdict = judge_verdict
   60:         self._mirror_fail_closed = mirror_fail_closed
   61:         self.seen_roles: list[str] = []
   62: 
   63:     def complete(self, request: RoleRequest) -> RoleResponse:
   64:         self.seen_roles.append(request.role)
   65:         if request.role == "mirror":
   66:             if "pass2_input" in request.params:
   67:                 content_hash = request.params["pass2_input"]["content_hash"]
   68:                 payload = {"content_hash": content_hash, "classification": "supported"}
   69:                 return RoleResponse(
   70:                     raw_text=json.dumps(payload), served_model=request.model_slug
   71:                 )
   72:             # pass-1: managed citation path. Grounded -> doc1 (in evidence); fail-closed ->
   73:             # a hallucinated doc_id never supplied, which the binding guard rejects whole.
   74:             doc_id = "ghost-doc" if self._mirror_fail_closed else "doc1"
   75:             return RoleResponse(
   76:                 raw_text="grounded answer",
   77:                 served_model=request.model_slug,
   78:                 citations=[CitationSpan(span_start=0, span_end=8, doc_ids=(doc_id,))],
   79:             )
   80:         if request.role == "sentinel":
   81:             score = "no" if self._sentinel_grounded else "yes"
   82:             return RoleResponse(
   83:                 raw_text=f"<score>{score}</score>", served_model=request.model_slug
   84:             )
   85:         if request.role == "judge":
   86:             return RoleResponse(
   87:                 raw_text=self._judge_verdict, served_model=request.model_slug
   88:             )
   89:         raise AssertionError(f"unexpected role {request.role!r}")
   90: 
   91: 
   92: def _run(transport, *, claim_id="claim-1", severity="S0", s0_categories=None):
   93:     return run_claim_pipeline(
   94:         transport,
   95:         claim_id=claim_id,
   96:         claim="The dose is 5.0 mg.",
   97:         evidence_documents=_EVIDENCE,
   98:         severity=severity,
   99:         s0_categories=s0_categories or [],
  100:         model_slugs=_MODEL_SLUGS,
  101:         timestamp=_TIMESTAMP,
  102:     )
  103: 
  104: 
  105: # --- RecordingTransport: appends the served record BEFORE returning to the caller/adapter ---
  106: def test_recording_transport_records_before_returning() -> None:
  107:     # The wrapper must have appended the record by the time complete() returns, so a downstream
  108:     # adapter that parses/raises on the returned response cannot drop the served-identity record.
  109:     # (The end-to-end "record survives an adapter raise" guarantee is asserted by
  110:     # test_mirror_fail_closed_unsupported_and_record_present below.)
  111:     class _Inner:
  112:         def complete(self, request: RoleRequest) -> RoleResponse:
  113:             return RoleResponse(raw_text="x", served_model="served-x")
  114: 
  115:     rec = RecordingTransport(_Inner())
  116:     resp = rec.complete(RoleRequest(role="mirror", model_slug="cohere/command-a-plus"))
  117:     assert resp.served_model == "served-x"
  118:     assert len(rec.records) == 1
  119:     assert rec.records[0].role == "mirror"
  120:     assert rec.records[0].served_model == "served-x"
  121:     assert rec.records[0].parsed is None  # wrapper does not parse
  122: 
  123: 
  124: # --- ordering: Mirror -> Sentinel -> Judge ---
  125: def test_ordering_mirror_sentinel_judge() -> None:
  126:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=True, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  127:     _run(transport)
  128:     # Mirror is two passes; the first three DISTINCT roles in order must be mirror,sentinel,judge.
  129:     first_seen_order = []
  130:     for role in transport.seen_roles:
  131:         if role not in first_seen_order:
  132:             first_seen_order.append(role)
  133:     assert first_seen_order == ["mirror", "sentinel", "judge"]
  134: 
  135: 
  136: # --- happy path: Sentinel grounded + Judge VERIFIED -> final VERIFIED ---
  137: def test_grounded_verified_passes_through() -> None:
  138:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=True, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  139:     result = _run(transport)
  140:     assert result.raw_judge_verdict == "VERIFIED"
  141:     assert result.final_verdict == "VERIFIED"
  142:     assert result.d8_row.verdict == "VERIFIED"
  143: 
  144: 
  145: # --- Sentinel UNGROUNDED overrides Judge VERIFIED -> UNSUPPORTED (raw preserved) ---
  146: def test_sentinel_ungrounded_overrides_judge_verified() -> None:
  147:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=False, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  148:     result = _run(transport)
  149:     assert result.raw_judge_verdict == "VERIFIED"  # raw preserved
  150:     assert result.final_verdict == "UNSUPPORTED"   # overridden
  151:     assert result.d8_row.verdict == "UNSUPPORTED"
  152: 
  153: 
  154: # --- Sentinel UNGROUNDED PRESERVES a worse Judge FABRICATED (never upgraded to UNSUPPORTED) ---
  155: def test_sentinel_ungrounded_preserves_judge_fabricated() -> None:
  156:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=False, judge_verdict="FABRICATED")
  157:     result = _run(transport)
  158:     assert result.raw_judge_verdict == "FABRICATED"
  159:     assert result.final_verdict == "FABRICATED"  # NOT upgraded to UNSUPPORTED
  160:     assert result.d8_row.verdict == "FABRICATED"
  161: 
  162: 
  163: # --- Mirror fail-closed -> final UNSUPPORTED AND its served record still present ---
  164: def test_mirror_fail_closed_unsupported_and_record_present() -> None:
  165:     transport = MockTransport(mirror_fail_closed=True, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  166:     result = _run(transport)
  167:     assert result.final_verdict == "UNSUPPORTED"
  168:     assert result.d8_row.verdict == "UNSUPPORTED"
  169:     # Judge never ran on the short-circuit path.
  170:     assert result.raw_judge_verdict is None
  171:     assert result.judge_result is None
  172:     assert result.mirror_result is None  # Mirror failed closed
  173:     assert result.sentinel_result is None  # short-circuited
  174:     # The Mirror pass-1 served-identity record is STILL captured (recorded before the raise).
  175:     mirror_records = [r for r in result.records if r.role == "mirror"]
  176:     assert mirror_records, "Mirror served-identity record must survive fail-closed"
  177:     assert mirror_records[0].served_model == "cohere/command-a-plus"
  178:     # And no sentinel/judge call was made (short-circuit).
  179:     assert "sentinel" not in {r.role for r in result.records}
  180:     assert "judge" not in {r.role for r in result.records}
  181: 
  182: 
  183: # --- claim_id flows VERBATIM into the D8 row (never synthesized) ---
  184: def test_claim_id_flows_into_d8_row() -> None:
  185:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=True, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  186:     result = _run(transport, claim_id="custom-claim-id-xyz")
  187:     assert result.d8_row.claim_id == "custom-claim-id-xyz"
  188: 
  189: 
  190: # --- citation_id is harvested from the Mirror grounded span on the success path ---
  191: def test_citation_id_from_grounded_span() -> None:
  192:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=True, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  193:     result = _run(transport)
  194:     assert result.d8_row.citation_id == "doc1"
  195: 
  196: 
  197: # --- records capture the full served-identity trail on the success path (no blind spot) ---
  198: def test_records_complete_on_success() -> None:
  199:     transport = MockTransport(sentinel_grounded=True, judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  200:     result = _run(transport)
  201:     roles = [r.role for r in result.records]
  202:     # mirror pass-1 + pass-2 (2x) + sentinel (1x) + judge (1x) = 4 records.
  203:     assert roles.count("mirror") == 2
  204:     assert roles.count("sentinel") == 1
  205:     assert roles.count("judge") == 1

  207:

  209: # --- Sentinel parse-failure (parsed_ok False) is treated as UNSAFE -> downgrade VERIFIED ---
  210: def test_sentinel_unparsed_is_unsafe_override() -> None:
  211:     class _BadSentinel(MockTransport):
  212:         def complete(self, request: RoleRequest) -> RoleResponse:
  213:             if request.role == "sentinel":
  214:                 self.seen_roles.append(request.role)
  215:                 # Malformed -> parse fails closed (parsed_ok False, UNGROUNDED).
  216:                 return RoleResponse(raw_text="garbage", served_model=request.model_slug)
  217:             return super().complete(request)
  218: 
  219:     transport = _BadSentinel(judge_verdict="VERIFIED")
  220:     result = _run(transport)
  221:     assert result.sentinel_result is not None
  222:     assert result.sentinel_result.parsed_ok is False
  223:     assert result.final_verdict == "UNSUPPORTED"  # unparsed sentinel downgrades VERIFIED

docs\transparency.md:62:- T1 corpus endpoints — `fda.gov`, `accessdata.fda.gov`, `clinicaltrials.gov`, `ncbi.nlm.nih.gov`, `pmc.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov`, `pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov`, `ema.europa.eu`, `nice.org.uk`, `mhra.gov.uk`, `www.gov.uk`, `canada.ca`, `hc-sc.gc.ca`, `recalls-rappels.canada.ca`, `health-products.canada.ca`, `hres.ca`, `cda-amc.ca`, `who.int`, `iarc.who.int`
docs\transparency.md:70:What Serper receives: the search query string itself, plus the normal request metadata any HTTP API call carries — the API account/key, source IP, timestamp, and user-agent — which Serper's privacy policy (serper.dev/privacy) describes it logging as system/access activity. What Serper does NOT receive: the uploaded corpus, the evidence pool, the generated report, or any operator-entered content. Serper returns only result URLs + snippets; POLARIS then fetches the actual T1 evidence directly from the government corpus endpoints listed above.
docs\transparency.md:72:The rationale for accepting the exception: POLARIS's sovereignty constraint protects the **LLM inference path and the generated report data**. The orchestrator + report data run on Canadian/non-US infrastructure (Vexxhost / OVH Québec); the LLM inference path is *designed* for the sovereign OVH H200 vLLM endpoint but **currently routes via OpenRouter (US, transitional — see the egress entry above)** until the sovereign GPU cluster is brought up at the Session-A window. That transitional US dependency is the one inference-path exception, disclosed here and surfaced in-product. A web-search query is a short keyword string carrying no confidential research content; the sensitive artifact is the synthesized report, which never transits Serper. A reviewer who wants zero US touch in the search path can swap Serper for a non-US provider (Mojeek UK / Qwant FR / Ecosia DE) — the retrieval code is provider-shaped — but that is not required for the sovereignty posture as scoped.
docs\transparency.md:76:**No AWS endpoints.** SSM, EC2 messages, and S3 hosts are explicitly NOT in the allowlist (per I-carney-008 sovereignty audit).

docs\process\polaris_task_cycle_proposal_v2_delta_2026_05_28.md:40:**v2 revision:** the gate verdict is read **from the verdict file on disk**, mirroring `codex-required.yml:189-203` exactly: `grep -E '^verdict:[[:space:]]+(APPROVE|REQUEST_CHANGES)$' <gateFile> | tail -1`, exact-equality compare to `verdict: APPROVE`. Implementation: a `parseFinalVerdictFromFile(path)` helper reads `${gateFile}` (the file `codex exec > gateFile` wrote), greps the LAST matching line, returns APPROVE/REQUEST_CHANGES/NULL. The agent's `r.text` is used ONLY to confirm the file was written; it is NEVER the verdict source. If no final verdict line exists → hard error (do not advance iter).
